```
    pass('F', 'Contents hub вҖ” contains deep crawlable links', `${deepLinks.length} links`);
  }

  // Locale links must stay in locale
  const enLinks = allLinks.filter(href => href && (href.startsWith('/en/') || href.startsWith('https://kspiritsclub.com/en/')));
  const koLinksOnEn = allLinks.filter(href => href && (href.startsWith('/ko/') || href.startsWith('https://kspiritsclub.com/ko/')));
  if (koLinksOnEn.length > 0) {
    warn('F', 'EN contents hub вҖ” has links pointing to /ko/ paths', koLinksOnEn.slice(0, 3).join(', '));
  } else {
    pass('F', 'EN contents hub вҖ” locale links stay in /en/');
  }

  // Wiki hub must have links to individual category pages
  const wikiUrl = `${BASE_URL}/en/contents/wiki`;
  const wikiResult = await fetchPage(wikiUrl);
  if (wikiResult.ok && wikiResult.status === 200) {
    const $w = parseHtml(wikiResult.html);
    const wikiCategoryLinks = $w('a[href]').filter((_, el) => {
      const href = $w(el).attr('href') || '';
      return /\/contents\/wiki\/[^/]+/.test(href);
    });
    if (wikiCategoryLinks.length === 0) {
      fail('F', 'Wiki hub вҖ” no crawlable links to category pages found');
    } else {
      pass('F', 'Wiki hub вҖ” crawlable category links present', `${wikiCategoryLinks.length} links`);
    }
  }
}

// в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
// G. Private/auth route safety (code inspection вҖ” no login required)
// в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

function readSourceFile(relPath) {
  const absPath = path.join(REPO_ROOT, relPath);
  try {
    return fs.readFileSync(absPath, 'utf-8');
  } catch {
    return null;
  }
}

/**
 * Returns true if a source file signals noindex via any of the standard patterns:
 *   robots: { index: false, ... }
 *   robots: { noindex: true }
 *   "noindex" string literal (robots meta string)
 */
function hasNoindexInSource(src) {
  return (
    /robots.*noindex/i.test(src) ||
    /noindex.*true/i.test(src) ||
    /index:\s*false/i.test(src)
  );
}

async function checkPrivateRouteSafety() {
  console.log('\nв”Җв”Җв”Җ G. Private/auth route safety (code inspection) в”Җв”Җв”Җ');

  // G1. robots.ts must block private paths at the crawl level
  const robotsSource = readSourceFile('app/robots.ts');
  if (!robotsSource) {
    fail('G', 'robots.ts source file not found');
  } else {
    const privatePaths = ['/ko/cabinet', '/en/cabinet', '/ko/me', '/en/me', '/ko/admin', '/en/admin'];
    for (const p of privatePaths) {
      if (robotsSource.includes(`'${p}'`) || robotsSource.includes(`"${p}"`)) {
        pass('G', `robots.ts disallows ${p}`);
      } else {
        fail('G', `robots.ts missing disallow for ${p}`);
      }
    }
  }

  // G2. sitemap.ts must not include private paths
  const sitemapSource = readSourceFile('app/sitemap.ts');
  if (!sitemapSource) {
    fail('G', 'sitemap.ts source file not found');
  } else {
    const bannedInSitemap = ['/cabinet', '/me', '/admin'];
    for (const p of bannedInSitemap) {
      // Look for path literal being added to routes array
      const leakPattern = new RegExp(`path:\\s*['"\`].*${p.replace('/', '\\/')}`, 'i');
      if (leakPattern.test(sitemapSource)) {
        fail('G', `sitemap.ts appears to include private path ${p}`);
      } else {
        pass('G', `sitemap.ts does not include private path ${p}`);
      }
    }
    // Confirm private pages comment is present (documentation guard)
    if (/NON-INDEXABLE|cabinet.*excluded|private/i.test(sitemapSource)) {
      pass('G', 'sitemap.ts has documented exclusion comment for private pages');
    } else {
      warn('G', 'sitemap.ts missing explicit comment about private page exclusion');
    }
  }

  // G3. Cabinet page must not have robots: { index: true }
  const cabinetSource = readSourceFile('app/[lang]/cabinet/page.tsx');
  if (!cabinetSource) {
    warn('G', 'Cabinet page source not found вҖ” skipping');
  } else {
    // Match only "index: true" (not "index: false" followed by "follow: true")
    if (/index\s*:\s*true/i.test(cabinetSource) && !/index\s*:\s*false/i.test(cabinetSource)) {
      fail('G', 'Cabinet page вҖ” explicitly sets robots index:true (should not be publicly indexable)');
    } else {
      pass('G', 'Cabinet page вҖ” does not explicitly set robots index:true');
    }
    // G3b. Cabinet page should have explicit noindex
    if (/index\s*:\s*false/i.test(cabinetSource)) {
      pass('G', 'Cabinet page вҖ” has explicit robots noindex');
    } else {
      fail('G', 'Cabinet page вҖ” missing explicit robots noindex (private page must be noindex)');
    }
    // Cabinet page should not have public-style meta description (generic site desc is fine)
    if (/generateMetadata/i.test(cabinetSource)) {
      pass('G', 'Cabinet page вҖ” has generateMetadata function');
    }
    // Check that the canonical is for /cabinet, not a public page path
    if (cabinetSource.includes('/cabinet')) {
      pass('G', 'Cabinet page вҖ” canonical references /cabinet path');
    } else {
      warn('G', 'Cabinet page вҖ” canonical path may not reference /cabinet');
    }
  }

  // G4. Me (profile) page must not have robots: { index: true }
  const meSource = readSourceFile('app/[lang]/me/page.tsx');
  if (!meSource) {
    warn('G', 'Me/profile page source not found вҖ” skipping');
  } else {
    // Match only "index: true" (not "index: false" followed by "follow: true")
    if (/index\s*:\s*true/i.test(meSource) && !/index\s*:\s*false/i.test(meSource)) {
      fail('G', 'Me page вҖ” explicitly sets robots index:true (should not be publicly indexable)');
    } else {
      pass('G', 'Me page вҖ” does not explicitly set robots index:true');
    }
    // G4b. Me page should have explicit noindex
    if (/index\s*:\s*false/i.test(meSource)) {
      pass('G', 'Me page вҖ” has explicit robots noindex');
    } else {
      fail('G', 'Me page вҖ” missing explicit robots noindex (private page must be noindex)');
    }
  }

  // G5. Verify the indexable-tier utility is used (not bypassed) in spirit pages
  const spiritPageSource = readSourceFile('app/[lang]/spirits/[id]/page.tsx');
  if (!spiritPageSource) {
    warn('G', 'Spirit detail page source not found вҖ” skipping');
  } else {
    if (/isIndexableSpirit|getSpiritRobotsMeta|FOUND_INDEXABLE|isIndexable/i.test(spiritPageSource)) {
      pass('G', 'Spirit page вҖ” uses indexable-tier classification');
    } else {
      fail('G', 'Spirit page вҖ” does not appear to use indexable-tier classification (regression risk)');
    }
    // Must set robots: noindex for Tier B spirits
    if (/robots.*index.*false|noindex/i.test(spiritPageSource)) {
      pass('G', 'Spirit page вҖ” has noindex path for thin content');
    } else {
      fail('G', 'Spirit page вҖ” no noindex code path found for thin spirits');
    }
  }

  // G6. Contact page must have noindex
  const contactSource = readSourceFile('app/[lang]/contents/contact/page.tsx');
  if (!contactSource) {
    warn('G', 'Contact page source not found вҖ” skipping');
  } else {
    if (hasNoindexInSource(contactSource)) {
      pass('G', 'Contact page вҖ” has noindex');
    } else {
      fail('G', 'Contact page вҖ” missing noindex (utility page should not be indexed)');
    }
  }

  // G7. Terms and privacy pages вҖ” should have noindex
  for (const utilityPage of ['terms', 'privacy']) {
    const src = readSourceFile(`app/[lang]/contents/${utilityPage}/page.tsx`);
    if (!src) {
      warn('G', `${utilityPage} page source not found вҖ” skipping`);
      continue;
    }
    if (hasNoindexInSource(src)) {
      pass('G', `${utilityPage} page вҖ” has noindex`);
    } else {
      warn('G', `${utilityPage} page вҖ” no explicit noindex found (utility page may be indexed)`);
    }
  }

  // G8. seo-url.ts utility must be used by main page types (shared code guard)
  const seoUrlSource = readSourceFile('lib/utils/seo-url.ts');
  if (!seoUrlSource) {
    fail('G', 'lib/utils/seo-url.ts not found вҖ” SEO URL utility missing');
  } else {
    pass('G', 'lib/utils/seo-url.ts exists');
    // Verify getCanonicalUrl and getHreflangAlternates are exported
    if (/export.*getCanonicalUrl/.test(seoUrlSource) && /export.*getHreflangAlternates/.test(seoUrlSource)) {
      pass('G', 'seo-url.ts exports getCanonicalUrl and getHreflangAlternates');
    } else {
      fail('G', 'seo-url.ts missing expected exports');
    }
  }

  // G9. Key public pages must import from seo-url (guard against refactor regression)
  const seoUrlUsers = [
    { file: 'app/[lang]/contents/reviews/page.tsx', label: 'Reviews page' },
    { file: 'app/[lang]/contents/news/page.tsx', label: 'News page' },
    { file: 'app/[lang]/contents/wiki/page.tsx', label: 'Wiki hub page' },
    { file: 'app/[lang]/contents/page.tsx', label: 'Contents hub page' },
  ];
  for (const { file, label } of seoUrlUsers) {
    const src = readSourceFile(file);
    if (!src) {
      warn('G', `${label} source not found вҖ” skipping seo-url import check`);
    } else if (/from.*seo-url/.test(src)) {
      pass('G', `${label} вҖ” imports from seo-url`);
    } else {
      fail('G', `${label} вҖ” does NOT import from seo-url (canonical/hreflang may be missing)`);
    }
  }
}

// в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
// H. Phase 7-2 Re-audit: DOM order, locale leakage, loading-shell, code guards
// в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

/**
 * Korean taxonomy/value strings that must NOT appear in the visible text of
 * EN-locale pages. These are short-form category keys used in the database
 * that would be returned as-is when no EN mapping existed (locale leakage).
 *
 * Note: Common product-name terms like 'мҶҢмЈј' are intentionally excluded
 * because they appear legitimately as Korean product names on EN pages.
 * This list covers categories that have unambiguous English equivalents and
 * should never appear as raw Korean strings in EN routes.
 */
const KO_TAXONOMY_LEAK_PATTERNS = [
  /\bлІ„лІҲ\b/,
  /\bлҚ°нӮ¬лқј\b/,
  /\bл©”мҠӨм№ј\b/,
  /\bмҮјм¶”\b/,
  /\bл Ҳл“ңмҷҖмқё\b/,
  /\bнҷ”мқҙнҠёмҷҖмқё\b/,
  /\bлҰ¬нҒҗм–ҙ\b/,
  /\bл°ұмЈј\b/,
];

async function checkPhase72() {
  console.log('\nв”Җв”Җв”Җ H. Phase 7-2 Re-audit в”Җв”Җв”Җ');

  // в”Җв”Җ H1. DOM order: <main> must appear before <footer> in the HTML в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  const domOrderPages = [
    { path: '/en', label: 'English homepage' },
    { path: '/ko', label: 'Korean homepage' },
  ];

  for (const page of domOrderPages) {
    const url = `${BASE_URL}${page.path}`;
    const result = await fetchPage(url);
    if (!result.ok || result.status !== 200) {
      warn('H', `${page.label} DOM order вҖ” could not verify (status ${result.status})`);
      continue;
    }

    const html = result.html;
    const mainIdx = html.indexOf('<main');
    const footerIdx = html.indexOf('<footer');

    if (mainIdx === -1) {
      fail('H', `${page.label} вҖ” no <main> element found in HTML`);
    } else if (footerIdx === -1) {
      warn('H', `${page.label} вҖ” no <footer> element found (cannot verify DOM order)`);
    } else if (mainIdx < footerIdx) {
      pass('H', `${page.label} вҖ” <main> appears before <footer> in DOM`);
    } else {
      fail('H', `${page.label} вҖ” <footer> appears before <main> in DOM (SEO structure issue)`,
        `main at char ${mainIdx}, footer at char ${footerIdx}`);
    }
  }

  // в”Җв”Җ H2. Loading-shell leakage on spirit detail (EN) в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  const indexableId = FIXTURES.indexableSpiritId;
  const spiritEnUrl = `${BASE_URL}/en/spirits/${indexableId}`;
  const spiritEnResult = await fetchPage(spiritEnUrl);

  if (!spiritEnResult.ok || spiritEnResult.status !== 200) {
    warn('H', `EN spirit (${indexableId}) вҖ” could not verify (status ${spiritEnResult.status})`);
  } else {
    let leaked = null;
    for (const pattern of LOADING_SHELL_PATTERNS) {
      if (pattern.test(spiritEnResult.html)) { leaked = pattern.toString(); break; }
    }
    if (leaked) {
      fail('H', `EN spirit вҖ” loading-shell text in SSR HTML`, `Pattern: ${leaked}`);
    } else {
      pass('H', `EN spirit вҖ” no loading-shell text in SSR HTML`);
    }

    // H3. EN spirit page вҖ” Korean taxonomy strings must not appear in visible body text
    const $ = parseHtml(spiritEnResult.html);
    // Remove script/style content from body text inspection
    $('script, style, [type="application/ld+json"]').remove();
    const bodyText = $('body').text();

    let koLeakPattern = null;
    for (const pattern of KO_TAXONOMY_LEAK_PATTERNS) {
      if (pattern.test(bodyText)) { koLeakPattern = pattern.toString(); break; }
    }
    if (koLeakPattern) {
      warn('H', `EN spirit вҖ” Korean taxonomy string found in body text`, `Pattern: ${koLeakPattern}`);
    } else {
      pass('H', `EN spirit вҖ” no Korean taxonomy leakage in body text`);
    }
  }

  // в”Җв”Җ H4. EN spirit JSON-LD must not contain raw Korean category strings в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  if (spiritEnResult.ok && spiritEnResult.status === 200) {
    const $ = parseHtml(spiritEnResult.html);
    const jsonLdScripts = $('script[type="application/ld+json"]').map((_, el) => $(el).html()).get();
    let jsonLdKoLeak = false;
    for (const scriptContent of jsonLdScripts) {
      try {
        const parsed = JSON.parse(scriptContent || '{}');
        const jsonStr = JSON.stringify(parsed);
        for (const pattern of KO_TAXONOMY_LEAK_PATTERNS) {
          if (pattern.test(jsonStr)) { jsonLdKoLeak = true; break; }
        }
      } catch { /* ignore parse errors */ }
      if (jsonLdKoLeak) break;
    }
    if (jsonLdKoLeak) {
      warn('H', `EN spirit вҖ” Korean taxonomy string found in JSON-LD structured data`);
    } else {
      pass('H', `EN spirit вҖ” no Korean taxonomy leakage in JSON-LD`);
    }
  }

  // в”Җв”Җ H5. Reviews archive must not expose loading shell text в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  const reviewsResult = await fetchPage(`${BASE_URL}/en/contents/reviews`);
  if (reviewsResult.ok && reviewsResult.status === 200) {
    let leaked = null;
    for (const pattern of LOADING_SHELL_PATTERNS) {
      if (pattern.test(reviewsResult.html)) { leaked = pattern.toString(); break; }
    }
    if (leaked) {
      fail('H', `Reviews archive вҖ” loading-shell text in SSR HTML`, `Pattern: ${leaked}`);
    } else {
      pass('H', `Reviews archive вҖ” no loading-shell text in SSR HTML`);
    }
  } else {
    warn('H', `Reviews archive вҖ” could not verify loading shell (status ${reviewsResult.status})`);
  }

  // в”Җв”Җ H6. News archive must not expose loading shell text в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  const newsResult = await fetchPage(`${BASE_URL}/en/contents/news`);
  if (newsResult.ok && newsResult.status === 200) {
    let leaked = null;
    for (const pattern of LOADING_SHELL_PATTERNS) {
      if (pattern.test(newsResult.html)) { leaked = pattern.toString(); break; }
    }
    if (leaked) {
      fail('H', `News archive вҖ” loading-shell text in SSR HTML`, `Pattern: ${leaked}`);
    } else {
      pass('H', `News archive вҖ” no loading-shell text in SSR HTML`);
    }
  } else {
    warn('H', `News archive вҖ” could not verify loading shell (status ${newsResult.status})`);
  }

  // в”Җв”Җ H7. Code guard: reviews-client and news-client must not start with loading=true в”Җ
  const reviewsClientSrc = readSourceFile('app/[lang]/contents/reviews/reviews-client.tsx');
  if (!reviewsClientSrc) {
    warn('H', 'reviews-client.tsx not found вҖ” skipping loading-shell guard');
  } else {
    // Must NOT have useState(!hasInitial) pattern (that would SSR the loading text)
    if (/useState\s*\(\s*!hasInitial\s*\)/.test(reviewsClientSrc)) {
      fail('H', 'reviews-client вҖ” loading state initialised to !hasInitial (SSR shell risk)',
        'Change to useState(false) so SSR never renders the loading placeholder text');
    } else {
      pass('H', 'reviews-client вҖ” loading state does not start from !hasInitial');
    }
  }

  const newsClientSrc = readSourceFile('app/[lang]/contents/news/news-client.tsx');
  if (!newsClientSrc) {
    warn('H', 'news-client.tsx not found вҖ” skipping loading-shell guard');
  } else {
    if (/useState\s*\(\s*!hasInitial\s*\)/.test(newsClientSrc)) {
      fail('H', 'news-client вҖ” loading state initialised to !hasInitial (SSR shell risk)',
        'Change to useState(false) so SSR never renders the loading placeholder text');
    } else {
      pass('H', 'news-client вҖ” loading state does not start from !hasInitial');
    }
  }

  // в”Җв”Җ H8. Code guard: spirit detail page uses localizeCategory for JSON-LD в”Җв”Җ
  const spiritPageSrc = readSourceFile('app/[lang]/spirits/[id]/page.tsx');
  if (!spiritPageSrc) {
    warn('H', 'Spirit detail page not found вҖ” skipping locale-leakage code guard');
  } else {
    // JSON-LD category must use localizeCategory or formatSpiritFieldValue, not raw spirit.category
    if (/category:\s*spirit\.category\b/.test(spiritPageSrc)) {
      fail('H', 'Spirit page вҖ” JSON-LD category uses raw spirit.category (Korean leak on EN routes)',
        'Use formatSpiritFieldValue(\'category\', spirit.category, lang) instead');
    } else if (/category:\s*localizeCategory/.test(spiritPageSrc) ||
               /category:\s*formatSpiritFieldValue/.test(spiritPageSrc)) {
      pass('H', 'Spirit page вҖ” JSON-LD category is localized');
    } else {
      warn('H', 'Spirit page вҖ” could not confirm JSON-LD category localization');
    }

    // buildRichDescription must be locale-aware (use isEn branching)
    if (/buildRichDescription/.test(spiritPageSrc) && /isEn/.test(spiritPageSrc)) {
      pass('H', 'Spirit page вҖ” buildRichDescription is locale-aware');
    } else {
      warn('H', 'Spirit page вҖ” buildRichDescription may not be locale-aware');
    }

    // Breadcrumb position 3 name must not be raw spirit.category
    if (/position:\s*3[\s\S]{0,100}name:\s*spirit\.category/.test(spiritPageSrc)) {
      fail('H', 'Spirit page вҖ” breadcrumb position 3 uses raw spirit.category (Korean leak on EN routes)',
        'Use localizeCategory(spirit.category, lang) for the breadcrumb name');
    } else {
      pass('H', 'Spirit page вҖ” breadcrumb position 3 does not use raw spirit.category');
    }
  }

  // в”Җв”Җ H9. display_names_en must include common short-form category keys в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  const metadataPath = path.join(REPO_ROOT, 'lib/constants/spirits-metadata.json');
  try {
    const metadataContent = fs.readFileSync(metadataPath, 'utf-8');
    const metadata = JSON.parse(metadataContent);
    const displayNamesEn = metadata.display_names_en || {};

    const requiredEnKeys = ['лІ„лІҲ', 'лҚ°нӮ¬лқј', 'л©”мҠӨм№ј', 'мҮјм¶”', 'л Ҳл“ңмҷҖмқё', 'нҷ”мқҙнҠёмҷҖмқё', 'лҰ¬нҒҗм–ҙ', 'л°ұмЈј'];
    const missingKeys = requiredEnKeys.filter(k => !displayNamesEn[k]);

    if (missingKeys.length > 0) {
      fail('H', 'spirits-metadata.json missing EN display names for short-form category keys',
        `Missing: ${missingKeys.join(', ')}`);
    } else {
      pass('H', 'spirits-metadata.json has EN display names for all short-form category keys');
    }
  } catch {
    warn('H', 'Could not read spirits-metadata.json for display_names_en check');
  }

  // в”Җв”Җ H10. Terms and privacy pages must have noindex в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  for (const page of ['terms', 'privacy']) {
    const src = readSourceFile(`app/[lang]/contents/${page}/page.tsx`);
    if (!src) {
      warn('H', `${page} page not found вҖ” skipping noindex guard`);
    } else if (hasNoindexInSource(src)) {
      pass('H', `${page} page вҖ” has noindex (utility page correctly excluded)`);
    } else {
      warn('H', `${page} page вҖ” missing noindex (utility page may be unnecessarily indexed)`);
    }
  }

  // в”Җв”Җ H11. Login page must have noindex в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  const loginSource = readSourceFile('app/[lang]/login/page.tsx');
  if (!loginSource) {
    warn('H', 'Login page source not found вҖ” skipping noindex guard');
  } else if (/index\s*:\s*false/i.test(loginSource)) {
    pass('H', 'Login page вҖ” has explicit robots noindex');
  } else {
    fail('H', 'Login page вҖ” missing explicit robots noindex (auth page should not be indexed)');
  }

  // в”Җв”Җ H12. Me/reviews must have noindex via layout or page metadata в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  const meReviewsLayout = readSourceFile('app/[lang]/me/reviews/layout.tsx');
  const meReviewsPage = readSourceFile('app/[lang]/me/reviews/page.tsx');
  const meReviewsNoindex =
    (meReviewsLayout && /index\s*:\s*false/i.test(meReviewsLayout)) ||
    (meReviewsPage && /index\s*:\s*false/i.test(meReviewsPage));
  if (meReviewsNoindex) {
    pass('H', 'Me/reviews вҖ” has explicit robots noindex');
  } else {
    fail('H', 'Me/reviews вҖ” missing robots noindex (private review page must be noindex)');
  }

  // в”Җв”Җ H13. About page must have locale-aware generateMetadata в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  const aboutSource = readSourceFile('app/[lang]/contents/about/page.tsx');
  if (!aboutSource) {
    warn('H', 'About page source not found вҖ” skipping locale-metadata guard');
  } else {
    // Must use a function (not static export const metadata) to be locale-aware
    const hasGenerateMetadata = /generateMetadata/i.test(aboutSource);
    // Must branch on locale (isEn pattern or direct lang comparison)
    const hasLocaleBranch = /\bisEn\b/.test(aboutSource) || /lang\s*===\s*['"]en['"]/.test(aboutSource);
    if (hasGenerateMetadata && hasLocaleBranch) {
      pass('H', 'About page вҖ” uses locale-aware generateMetadata');
    } else {
      fail('H', 'About page вҖ” static metadata is not locale-aware (KO route gets English title)');
    }
  }

  // в”Җв”Җ H14. Spirit page JSON-LD fallback must be locale-aware on EN routes в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  const spiritPageSrcH14 = readSourceFile('app/[lang]/spirits/[id]/page.tsx');
  if (!spiritPageSrcH14) {
    warn('H', 'Spirit detail page source not found вҖ” skipping JSON-LD fallback check');
  } else {
    // The fallback editorialReviewBody must reference isEn (locale-conditional) and
    // localizeCategory must be called with 'en' argument for the EN branch
    const fallbackIsLocaleAware = /editorialReviewBody\s*=.*isEn/s.test(spiritPageSrcH14) ||
      /isEn.*editorialReviewBody/s.test(spiritPageSrcH14);
    const localizeCalledWithEn = /localizeCategory\([^)]*'en'\)/.test(spiritPageSrcH14);
    if (fallbackIsLocaleAware || localizeCalledWithEn) {
      pass('H', 'Spirit page вҖ” JSON-LD editorial review fallback is locale-aware');
    } else {
      warn('H', 'Spirit page вҖ” JSON-LD editorial review fallback may not be locale-aware');
    }
  }

  // в”Җв”Җ H15. WorldCup layout must not have static Korean-only metadata в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  const worldcupLayoutSrc = readSourceFile('app/[lang]/contents/worldcup/layout.tsx');
  if (!worldcupLayoutSrc) {
    warn('H', 'WorldCup layout source not found вҖ” skipping metadata conflict check');
  } else if (/export const metadata/i.test(worldcupLayoutSrc)) {
    fail('H', 'WorldCup layout вҖ” has static metadata that conflicts with locale-aware page metadata');
  } else {
    pass('H', 'WorldCup layout вҖ” no static metadata (page handles locale-aware title)');
  }

  // в”Җв”Җ H16. WorldCup/game layout must use locale-aware generateMetadata в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  const worldcupGameLayoutSrc = readSourceFile('app/[lang]/contents/worldcup/game/layout.tsx');
  if (!worldcupGameLayoutSrc) {
    warn('H', 'WorldCup/game layout source not found вҖ” skipping metadata locale check');
  } else {
    const hasGenerateMetadata = /generateMetadata/i.test(worldcupGameLayoutSrc);
    const hasLocaleBranch = /\bisEn\b/.test(worldcupGameLayoutSrc) || /lang\s*===\s*['"]en['"]/.test(worldcupGameLayoutSrc);
    if (hasGenerateMetadata && hasLocaleBranch) {
      pass('H', 'WorldCup/game layout вҖ” uses locale-aware generateMetadata');
    } else {
      fail('H', 'WorldCup/game layout вҖ” has static Korean-only metadata (EN routes get Korean title)');
    }
  }

  // в”Җв”Җ H17. Perfect-pour layout must not have static Korean-only metadata в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  const perfectPourLayoutSrc = readSourceFile('app/[lang]/contents/perfect-pour/layout.tsx');
  if (!perfectPourLayoutSrc) {
    warn('H', 'Perfect-pour layout source not found вҖ” skipping metadata conflict check');
  } else if (/export const metadata/i.test(perfectPourLayoutSrc)) {
    fail('H', 'Perfect-pour layout вҖ” has static metadata that conflicts with locale-aware page metadata');
  } else {
    pass('H', 'Perfect-pour layout вҖ” no static metadata (page handles locale-aware title)');
  }

  // в”Җв”Җ H18. WorldCup result page must be locale-aware and explicitly noindex в”Җв”Җв”Җ
  const worldcupResultSrc = readSourceFile('app/[lang]/contents/worldcup/result/[id]/page.tsx');
  if (!worldcupResultSrc) {
    warn('H', 'WorldCup result page source not found вҖ” skipping locale/noindex guard');
  } else {
    const hasGenerateMetadata = /generateMetadata/i.test(worldcupResultSrc);
    const hasLocaleBranch = /\bisEn\b/.test(worldcupResultSrc) || /lang\s*===\s*['"]en['"]/.test(worldcupResultSrc);
    const hasLocalizedReturnLink = /href=\{`\/\$\{lang\}\/contents\/worldcup`\}/.test(worldcupResultSrc);

    if (hasGenerateMetadata && hasLocaleBranch) {
      pass('H', 'WorldCup result page вҖ” uses locale-aware generateMetadata');
    } else {
      fail('H', 'WorldCup result page вҖ” metadata is not locale-aware');
    }

    if (hasNoindexInSource(worldcupResultSrc)) {
      pass('H', 'WorldCup result page вҖ” has explicit robots noindex');
    } else {
      fail('H', 'WorldCup result page вҖ” missing robots noindex');
    }

    if (hasLocalizedReturnLink && !/href="\/contents\/worldcup"/.test(worldcupResultSrc)) {
      pass('H', 'WorldCup result page вҖ” uses locale-prefixed WorldCup links');
    } else {
      fail('H', 'WorldCup result page вҖ” contains locale-less WorldCup links');
    }
  }

  // в”Җв”Җ H19. Taste result page must be locale-aware and explicitly noindex в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  const tasteResultSrc = readSourceFile('app/[lang]/contents/taste/result/[userId]/page.tsx');
  if (!tasteResultSrc) {
    warn('H', 'Taste result page source not found вҖ” skipping locale/noindex guard');
  } else {
    const hasGenerateMetadata = /generateMetadata/i.test(tasteResultSrc);
    const hasLocaleBranch = /\bisEn\b/.test(tasteResultSrc) || /lang\s*===\s*['"]en['"]/.test(tasteResultSrc);

    if (hasGenerateMetadata && hasLocaleBranch) {
      pass('H', 'Taste result page вҖ” uses locale-aware generateMetadata');
    } else {
      fail('H', 'Taste result page вҖ” metadata is not locale-aware');
    }

    if (hasNoindexInSource(tasteResultSrc)) {
      pass('H', 'Taste result page вҖ” has explicit robots noindex');
    } else {
      fail('H', 'Taste result page вҖ” missing robots noindex');
    }
  }

  // в”Җв”Җ H20. WorldCup game page links must retain locale prefixes в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  const worldcupGamePageSrc = readSourceFile('app/[lang]/contents/worldcup/game/page.tsx');
  if (!worldcupGamePageSrc) {
    warn('H', 'WorldCup/game page source not found вҖ” skipping locale-link guard');
  } else {
    const hasLocalizedShareUrl = /window\.location\.origin\}\/\$\{lang\}\/contents\/worldcup\/result\/\$\{resultId\}/.test(worldcupGamePageSrc);
    const hasLocalizedRouterPush = /router\.push\(`\/\$\{lang\}\/contents\/worldcup`\)/.test(worldcupGamePageSrc);
    const hasLocaleLeak = /\/contents\/worldcup\/result\/\$\{resultId\}/.test(worldcupGamePageSrc) && !hasLocalizedShareUrl;

    if (hasLocalizedShareUrl && hasLocalizedRouterPush && !hasLocaleLeak) {
      pass('H', 'WorldCup/game page вҖ” share and navigation links retain locale prefixes');
    } else {
      fail('H', 'WorldCup/game page вҖ” locale-less share or navigation link detected');
    }
  }
}


// в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
// I. SSR / hydration parity
//
// Verifies that the SSR HTML and the final hydrated DOM contain the same
// localized field values вҖ” no raw Korean DB values on EN routes, no loading
// shell text, and metadata language matches body language.
// в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

/**
 * Raw Korean country strings (DB abbreviations and full names) that must
 * never appear as-is in EN route JSON-LD or visible body text.
 * Shared by I4 (JSON-LD check) and I5 (body text check).
 */
const RAW_KO_COUNTRIES = ['мқј', 'мқјліё', 'лҢҖн•ңлҜјкөӯ', 'лҜёкөӯ', 'мҳҒкөӯ', 'мӨ‘көӯ', 'лҸ…мқј', 'н”„лһ‘мҠӨ', 'нҳёмЈј', 'мәҗлӮҳлӢӨ'];

/** Pre-compiled boundary regexes for the RAW_KO_COUNTRIES list (I5 body text check). */
const RAW_KO_COUNTRY_REGEXES = RAW_KO_COUNTRIES.map(ko => new RegExp(`(^|\\s|>)${ko}(\\s|<|$)`));

async function checkSsrParity(isOnline) {
  console.log('\nв”Җв”Җв”Җ I. SSR / hydration parity в”Җв”Җв”Җ');

  // в”Җв”Җ I1. Code guard: page.tsx must use localizeCountry in JSON-LD additionalProperty в”Җв”Җ
  const spiritPageSrc = readSourceFile('app/[lang]/spirits/[id]/page.tsx');
  if (!spiritPageSrc) {
    warn('I', 'Spirit page source not found вҖ” skipping SSR parity code guard');
  } else {
    // The additionalProperty block must NOT use raw spirit.country
    if (/additionalProperty[\s\S]{0,400}value:\s*spirit\.country\b/.test(spiritPageSrc)) {
      fail('I', 'Spirit page вҖ” JSON-LD additionalProperty.Country uses raw spirit.country (locale leak)',
        'Replace with localizeCountry(spirit.country, lang)');
    } else if (/additionalProperty[\s\S]{0,400}localizeCountry/.test(spiritPageSrc) ||
               /additionalProperty[\s\S]{0,400}formatSpiritFieldValue/.test(spiritPageSrc)) {
      pass('I', 'Spirit page вҖ” JSON-LD additionalProperty.Country is localized');
    } else {
      warn('I', 'Spirit page вҖ” could not confirm JSON-LD additionalProperty.Country localization');
    }
  }

  // в”Җв”Җ I2. Code guard: spirit-detail-client.tsx must use formatSpiritFieldValue в”Җв”Җ
  const clientSrc = readSourceFile('app/[lang]/spirits/[id]/spirit-detail-client.tsx');
  if (!clientSrc) {
    warn('I', 'spirit-detail-client.tsx not found вҖ” skipping spec table code guard');
  } else {
    if (/formatSpiritFieldValue/.test(clientSrc)) {
      pass('I', 'spirit-detail-client вҖ” spec table uses formatSpiritFieldValue');
    } else if (/getLocalizedCategory/.test(clientSrc)) {
      fail('I', 'spirit-detail-client вҖ” uses local getLocalizedCategory instead of formatSpiritFieldValue',
        'Replace getLocalizedCategory with formatSpiritFieldValue from localize-field.ts');
    } else {
      warn('I', 'spirit-detail-client вҖ” could not confirm spec table uses formatSpiritFieldValue');
    }
    // Must not import metadata directly for display_names (should go through formatSpiritFieldValue)
    if (/import metadata from.*spirits-metadata/.test(clientSrc) &&
        /display_names_en|display_names\b/.test(clientSrc)) {
      warn('I', 'spirit-detail-client вҖ” still accessing spirits-metadata.json display_names directly; prefer formatSpiritFieldValue');
    } else {
      pass('I', 'spirit-detail-client вҖ” does not bypass formatSpiritFieldValue for display names');
    }
  }

  // в”Җв”Җ I3. Code guard: formatSpiritFieldValue is exported from localize-field.ts в”Җв”Җ
  const localizeSrc = readSourceFile('lib/utils/localize-field.ts');
  if (!localizeSrc) {
    fail('I', 'lib/utils/localize-field.ts not found');
  } else {
    if (/export function formatSpiritFieldValue/.test(localizeSrc)) {
      pass('I', 'localize-field.ts exports formatSpiritFieldValue');
    } else {
      fail('I', 'localize-field.ts missing formatSpiritFieldValue export',
        'Add the unified helper function so all consumers go through one entry-point');
    }
  }

  // в”Җв”Җ I9. Code guard: page.tsx must import formatSpiritFieldValue в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  const spiritPageSrcI9 = readSourceFile('app/[lang]/spirits/[id]/page.tsx');
  if (!spiritPageSrcI9) {
    warn('I', 'Spirit page source not found вҖ” skipping formatSpiritFieldValue import guard');
  } else if (/import\s*\{[^}]*formatSpiritFieldValue[^}]*\}/.test(spiritPageSrcI9)) {
    pass('I', 'Spirit page вҖ” imports formatSpiritFieldValue (unified localization helper)');
  } else if (/localizeCategory/.test(spiritPageSrcI9) || /localizeCountry/.test(spiritPageSrcI9)) {
    warn('I', 'Spirit page вҖ” uses localizeCategory/localizeCountry directly; migrate to formatSpiritFieldValue for SSR parity');
  } else {
    warn('I', 'Spirit page вҖ” could not confirm use of a localization helper in metadata/JSON-LD');
  }

  if (!isOnline) {
    warn('I', 'Server not reachable вҖ” skipping runtime SSR parity checks');
    return;
  }

  // в”Җв”Җ I4. Runtime: EN spirit JSON-LD additionalProperty.Country must be English в”Җв”Җ
  const indexableId = FIXTURES.indexableSpiritId;
  const spiritEnResult = await fetchPage(`${BASE_URL}/en/spirits/${indexableId}`);
  if (!spiritEnResult.ok || spiritEnResult.status !== 200) {
    warn('I', `EN spirit (${indexableId}) SSR parity вҖ” skipped (status ${spiritEnResult.status})`);
  } else {
    const $ = parseHtml(spiritEnResult.html);
    const jsonLdScripts = $('script[type="application/ld+json"]').map((_, el) => $(el).html()).get();

    let countryRawKoFound = false;
    let countryEnFound = false;

    for (const scriptContent of jsonLdScripts) {
      try {
        const parsed = JSON.parse(scriptContent || '{}');
        if (parsed.additionalProperty) {
          for (const prop of parsed.additionalProperty) {
            if (prop.name === 'Country') {
              if (RAW_KO_COUNTRIES.includes(prop.value)) {
                countryRawKoFound = true;
              } else if (prop.value && /^[A-Za-z\s]+$/.test(prop.value)) {
                countryEnFound = true;
              }
            }
          }
        }
      } catch (e) {
        // Ignore JSON parse errors in script blocks вҖ” malformed LD+JSON is
        // reported by other checks (H4); here we only care about localization.
      }
    }

    if (countryRawKoFound) {
      fail('I', 'EN spirit вҖ” JSON-LD additionalProperty.Country contains raw Korean country code',
        'Ensure localizeCountry(spirit.country, lang) is applied in JSON-LD generation');
    } else if (countryEnFound) {
      pass('I', 'EN spirit вҖ” JSON-LD additionalProperty.Country is English');
    } else {
      warn('I', 'EN spirit вҖ” could not verify JSON-LD additionalProperty.Country (field may be absent)');
    }

    // в”Җв”Җ I5. Runtime: EN spirit body text must contain localized category/country values в”Җв”Җ
    $('script, style, [type="application/ld+json"]').remove();
    const bodyText = $('body').text();

    // Spot-check: raw Korean country abbreviations must not appear in the visible body
    const rawKoInBody = RAW_KO_COUNTRY_REGEXES.some(re => re.test(bodyText));
    if (rawKoInBody) {
      warn('I', 'EN spirit вҖ” raw Korean country code found in visible body text');
    } else {
      pass('I', 'EN spirit вҖ” no raw Korean country codes in visible body text');
    }
  }

  // в”Җв”Җ I6. Runtime: Reviews archive must SSR at least one review item в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  const reviewsResult = await fetchPage(`${BASE_URL}/en/contents/reviews`);
  if (!reviewsResult.ok || reviewsResult.status !== 200) {
    warn('I', 'Reviews archive SSR вҖ” skipped (could not fetch)');
  } else {
    const $ = parseHtml(reviewsResult.html);
    // Reviews render spirit links in the list
    const spiritLinks = $('a[href*="/spirits/"]');
    if (spiritLinks.length === 0) {
      warn('I', 'Reviews archive вҖ” no spirit links found in SSR HTML (initialReviews may be empty or client-only)');
    } else {
      pass('I', 'Reviews archive вҖ” SSR contains spirit links', `${spiritLinks.length} links`);
    }
  }

  // в”Җв”Җ I7. Runtime: News archive must SSR at least one news item в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  const newsResult = await fetchPage(`${BASE_URL}/en/contents/news`);
  if (!newsResult.ok || newsResult.status !== 200) {
    warn('I', 'News archive SSR вҖ” skipped (could not fetch)');
  } else {
    const $ = parseHtml(newsResult.html);
    // News items render with article-style links
    const newsLinks = $('a[href]').filter((_, el) => {
      const href = $(el).attr('href') || '';
      return href.includes('/news/') || href.includes('/contents/news');
    });
    if (newsLinks.length <= 1) {
      warn('I', 'News archive вҖ” very few news links in SSR HTML (initialNews may be empty)');
    } else {
      pass('I', 'News archive вҖ” SSR contains news links', `${newsLinks.length} links`);
    }
  }

  // в”Җв”Җ I8. Runtime: Metadata language must match body language в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  const localePairs = [
    { path: `/en/spirits/${FIXTURES.indexableSpiritId}`, lang: 'en', label: `EN spirit (${FIXTURES.indexableSpiritId})` },
    { path: '/en/contents/reviews', lang: 'en', label: 'EN reviews' },
    { path: '/en/contents/news', lang: 'en', label: 'EN news' },
  ];

  for (const { path, lang, label } of localePairs) {
    const result = await fetchPage(`${BASE_URL}${path}`);
    if (!result.ok || result.status !== 200) {
      warn('I', `${label} metadata-body consistency вҖ” skipped (status ${result.status})`);
      continue;
    }
    const $ = parseHtml(result.html);
    const title = $('title').text().trim();
    const htmlLang = $('html').attr('lang') || '';

    // EN pages: html[lang] must be 'en' (or start with 'en')
    if (lang === 'en') {
      if (htmlLang.startsWith('en')) {
        pass('I', `${label} вҖ” html[lang] is correctly set to "${htmlLang}"`);
      } else if (htmlLang) {
        warn('I', `${label} вҖ” html[lang]="${htmlLang}" may not match page locale`, 'Expected en or en-*');
      } else {
        warn('I', `${label} вҖ” html[lang] attribute missing`);
      }
      // Title must not be purely Korean characters
      if (title && /^[к°Җ-нһЈ\sВ·\-()]+$/.test(title)) {
        fail('I', `${label} вҖ” title is Korean-only on an EN route (locale leak)`, title);
      } else if (title) {
        pass('I', `${label} вҖ” title language is consistent with EN route`);
      }
    }
  }

  // в”Җв”Җ I10. Runtime: EN spirit body must not contain raw Korean taxonomy values в”Җ
  /**
   * Korean category/subcategory keys from the spirits taxonomy that must never
   * appear untranslated in EN route body text. These map to English display names
   * via formatSpiritFieldValue('category', ...) / localizeCategory().
   */
  const RAW_KO_TAXONOMY = ['мҶҢмЈј', 'л§үкұёлҰ¬', 'мң„мҠӨнӮӨ', 'лІ„лІҲ', 'м§„', 'лҹј', 'ліҙл“ңм№ҙ', 'лҚ°нӮ¬лқј', 'мӮ¬мјҖ', 'мҮјм¶”', 'мҪ”лғ‘', 'лёҢлһңл””', 'м•ҪмЈј', 'мҷҖмқё', 'л§ҘмЈј', 'лҰ¬нҒҗм–ҙ'];
  /** Pre-compiled boundary regexes for RAW_KO_TAXONOMY (mirrors RAW_KO_COUNTRY_REGEXES pattern). */
  const RAW_KO_TAXONOMY_REGEXES = RAW_KO_TAXONOMY.map(ko => new RegExp(`(^|\\s|>)${ko}(\\s|<|$)`));
  if (!spiritEnResult.ok || spiritEnResult.status !== 200) {
    warn('I', 'EN spirit taxonomy SSR check вҖ” skipped (could not fetch spirit page)');
  } else {
    const $tx = parseHtml(spiritEnResult.html);
    $tx('script, style, [type="application/ld+json"]').remove();
    const bodyTextTx = $tx('body').text();
    const rawKoTaxonomyInBody = RAW_KO_TAXONOMY_REGEXES.some(re => re.test(bodyTextTx));
    if (rawKoTaxonomyInBody) {
      fail('I', 'EN spirit вҖ” raw Korean taxonomy category found in visible body text',
        'Ensure formatSpiritFieldValue is applied to all category/subcategory fields on EN routes');
    } else {
      pass('I', 'EN spirit вҖ” no raw Korean taxonomy categories in visible body text');
    }
  }

  // в”Җв”Җ I11. Runtime: Reviews archive SSR must contain вүҘ10 spirit links в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  if (!reviewsResult.ok || reviewsResult.status !== 200) {
    warn('I', 'Reviews archive SSR item count вҖ” skipped (could not fetch)');
  } else {
    const $rv = parseHtml(reviewsResult.html);
    const reviewSpiritLinks = $rv('a[href*="/spirits/"]');
    if (reviewSpiritLinks.length >= 10) {
      pass('I', 'Reviews archive вҖ” SSR contains вүҘ10 spirit card links', `${reviewSpiritLinks.length} links`);
    } else if (reviewSpiritLinks.length > 0) {
      warn('I', 'Reviews archive вҖ” SSR spirit link count below 10',
        `${reviewSpiritLinks.length} links found (expected вүҘ10 for full SSR coverage)`);
    } else {
      fail('I', 'Reviews archive вҖ” SSR must contain spirit card links (initialReviews empty or rendered client-only)',
        'Ensure reviewsDb.getLatest() returns data and passes it as initialReviews prop');
    }
  }

  // в”Җв”Җ I12. Runtime: News archive SSR must contain вүҘ10 news article elements в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  if (!newsResult.ok || newsResult.status !== 200) {
    warn('I', 'News archive SSR item count вҖ” skipped (could not fetch)');
  } else {
    const $nw = parseHtml(newsResult.html);
    const newsArticles = $nw('article');
    if (newsArticles.length >= 10) {
      pass('I', 'News archive вҖ” SSR contains вүҘ10 news articles', `${newsArticles.length} articles`);
    } else if (newsArticles.length > 0) {
      warn('I', 'News archive вҖ” SSR article count below 10',
        `${newsArticles.length} articles found (expected вүҘ10 for full SSR coverage)`);
    } else {
      fail('I', 'News archive вҖ” SSR must contain news article elements (initialNews empty or rendered client-only)',
        'Ensure newsDb.getLatest() returns data and passes it as initialNews prop');
    }
  }

  // в”Җв”Җ I13. Runtime: Spirit detail page must not expose loading-shell text in SSR в”Җ
  if (!spiritEnResult.ok || spiritEnResult.status !== 200) {
    warn('I', 'Spirit detail loading-shell check вҖ” skipped (could not fetch)');
  } else {
    let spiritShellLeak = null;
    for (const pattern of LOADING_SHELL_PATTERNS) {
      if (pattern.test(spiritEnResult.html)) {
        spiritShellLeak = pattern.toString();
        break;
      }
    }
    if (spiritShellLeak) {
      fail('I', 'Spirit detail вҖ” loading-shell text found in SSR HTML', `Pattern: ${spiritShellLeak}`);
    } else {
      pass('I', 'Spirit detail вҖ” no loading-shell text in SSR HTML');
    }
  }
}

function printSummary() {
  console.log('\n' + 'в•җ'.repeat(60));
  console.log('SEO Regression Check вҖ” Results');
  console.log('в•җ'.repeat(60));

  const grouped = {};
  for (const r of RESULTS) {
    if (!grouped[r.section]) grouped[r.section] = [];
    grouped[r.section].push(r);
  }

  for (const [section, items] of Object.entries(grouped)) {
    const fails = items.filter(i => i.level === 'FAIL');
    const warns = items.filter(i => i.level === 'WARN');
    const passes = items.filter(i => i.level === 'PASS');
    console.log(`\nSection ${section}: ${passes.length} PASS  ${warns.length} WARN  ${fails.length} FAIL`);
    for (const item of items) {
      const icon = item.level === 'PASS' ? 'вң…' : item.level === 'WARN' ? 'вҡ пёҸ ' : 'вқҢ';
      const detail = item.detail ? `  вҶ’ ${item.detail}` : '';
      console.log(`  ${icon} [${item.level}] ${item.label}${detail}`);
    }
  }

  console.log('\n' + 'в”Җ'.repeat(60));
  const total = RESULTS.length;
  const passCount = RESULTS.filter(r => r.level === 'PASS').length;
  console.log(`Total: ${total} checks  |  ${passCount} PASS  |  ${warnCount} WARN  |  ${blockerCount} FAIL (BLOCKER)`);

  if (blockerCount > 0) {
    console.log(`\nрҹҡЁ ${blockerCount} BLOCKER failure(s) detected. Fix before deploying.\n`);
  } else if (warnCount > 0) {
    console.log(`\nвң… No blockers. ${warnCount} warning(s) to review.\n`);
  } else {
    console.log('\nвң… All checks passed.\n');
  }
}

async function main() {
  console.log('K-Spirits Club вҖ” SEO Regression Check Suite');
  console.log(`BASE_URL: ${BASE_URL}`);
  console.log(`Fixtures: indexableSpiritId=${FIXTURES.indexableSpiritId}, missingSpiritId=${FIXTURES.missingSpiritId}`);

  // Always probe the target server regardless of URL вҖ” handles unreachable staging too
  const isOnline = await (async () => {
    try {
      await fetch(`${BASE_URL}/robots.txt`, { signal: AbortSignal.timeout(5000) });
      return true;
    } catch {
      return false;
    }
  })();

  if (!isOnline) {
    console.log(`\nвҡ пёҸ  Server not reachable at ${BASE_URL}. Skipping HTTP checks, running code-only checks.\n`);
    await checkPrivateRouteSafety();
    await checkPhase72();
    await checkSsrParity(false);
  } else {
    await checkPublicHtmlQuality();
    await checkMetadata();
    await checkSitemapRobots();
    await checkSpiritRoutes();
    await checkArchives();
    await checkCrawlableLinks();
    await checkPrivateRouteSafety();
    await checkPhase72();
    await checkSsrParity(true);
  }

  printSummary();
  process.exit(blockerCount > 0 ? 1 : 0);
}

main().catch(err => {
  console.error('Unexpected error:', err);
  process.exit(1);
});

```
